right2\n    print(f\"  After post-round diff: L diff={hex(left1 ^ left2)}, R diff={hex(right1 ^ right2)}\")\n    return right1, left1, right2, left2\n\nprint(\"\\nTracing diff:\")\ntrace_diff(P1, P2,
